class methods:

  1. character: aCharacter size: fontSize [accessing] 
     
	"ChemoJunHelvetica character: $C size: 12."

	aCharacter isAlphaNumeric 
		ifTrue: 
			[| aSymbol |
			aSymbol := ('image_' , (String with: aCharacter) , '_' 
						, fontSize printString) asSymbol.
			(self respondsTo: aSymbol) ifTrue: [^self perform: aSymbol]].
	^Image 
		extent: 0 @ 0
		depth: 24
		bitsPerPixel: 24
		palette: (Graphics.FixedPalette 
				redShift: 16
				redMask: 255
				greenShift: 8
				greenMask: 255
				blueShift: 0
				blueMask: 255)
  2. code: aCharacter size: fontSize [private] 
     
	"ChemoJunHelvetica character: $C size: 12."

	| aString composedText aPixmap graphicsContext figureImage fontModel textAttributes aStream aSelector |
	fontModel := JunFontModel new.
	fontModel fontName: 'helvetica'.
	fontModel fontSize: fontSize.
	textAttributes := fontModel textAttributes.
	aString := String with: aCharacter.
	composedText := ComposedText withText: aString asText style: textAttributes.
	aPixmap := Pixmap extent: composedText bounds extent.
	graphicsContext := aPixmap graphicsContext.
	graphicsContext paint: ColorValue white.
	graphicsContext displayRectangle: composedText bounds.
	graphicsContext paint: ColorValue black.
	composedText displayOn: graphicsContext.
	figureImage := aPixmap asImage.
	aPixmap close.
	figureImage := JunImageAdjuster convertTo24BitColorImage: figureImage.
	aSelector := 'image_' , aString , '_' , fontModel fontSize printString.
	aStream := String new writeStream.
	aStream nextPutAll: aSelector.
	aStream cr.
	aStream nextPutAll: '"' , self name , ' ' , aSelector , '."'.
	aStream cr.
	aStream nextPutAll: ' ^'.
	aStream nextPutAll: figureImage storeString.
	aString := aStream contents.
	aStream close.
	aString := Compiler new 
				format: aString
				in: self
				notifying: nil.
	^aString
  3. copyright [copyright] 
    	^'ChemoJun050 (2006/08/08) Copyright 2002-2006 National Institute of Informatics, Research Organization of Information and Systems.'
  4. generateMethods [private] 
    	"ChemoJunHelvetica generateMethods."

	| fontSizeCollection classifiedStringCollection |
	fontSizeCollection := #(7 9 10 12 14 18).
	classifiedStringCollection := fontSizeCollection collect: 
					[:n | 
					| aString |
					aString := n printString.
					2 - aString size timesRepeat: [aString := '0' , aString].
					aString yourself].
	fontSizeCollection with: classifiedStringCollection
		do: 
			[:fontSize :classifiedString | 
			'ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZabcdefghijklmnopqrstuvwxyz0123456789' do: 
					[:aCharacter | 
					| aCode |
					aCode := self code: aCharacter size: fontSize.
					self class compile: aCode classified: classifiedString]]
